                        "import os\nimport unittest\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\nfrom flask import Flask\nfrom flask_sqlalchemy import SQLAlchemy\n\n# Import the app and db from the code under test\n# Here we assume the code is in the same module, so we import app, db, and models directly.\n# If the code was in another file (e.g., ecommerce.py), you would do:\n# from ecommerce import app, db, User, Product, Order, OrderItem, create_jwt, ADMIN_EMAIL\n\n# For this test, we must redefine the models and app context as in the main code.\n# So, we will assume the code above is in the same file for simplicity.\n\n# --- Test Suite ---\n\nclass EcommerceTestCase(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Configure the app for testing\n        app.config['TESTING'] = True\n        app.config['SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI'] = 'sqlite:///:memory:'\n        app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'testsecret'\n        app.config['WTF_CSRF_ENABLED'] = False\n        self.app = app.test_client()\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.create_all()\n            # Create admin user\n            admin = User(\n                email=ADMIN_EMAIL,\n                password_hash=bcrypt.generate_password_hash(\"admin123\").decode('utf-8'),\n                is_admin=True\n            )\n            db.session.add(admin)\n            db.session.commit()\n            self.admin_id = admin.id\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        with app.app_context():\n            db.session.remove()\n            db.drop_all()\n\n    def register_user(self, email, password):\n        return self.app.post('/api/register', json={\n            'email': email,\n            'password': password\n        })\n\n    def login_user(self, email, password):\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'email': email,\n            'password': password\n        })\n        if resp.status_code == 200:\n            return json.loads(resp.data)['token']\n        return None\n\n    def create_product(self, token, name=\"Test Product\", price=10.0, stock=5):\n        return self.app.post('/api/admin/products', json={\n            \"name\": name,\n            \"description\": \"desc\",\n            \"price\": price,\n            \"image_url\": \"\",\n            \"stock\": stock\n        }, headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n\n    def test_registration_and_login(self):\n        # Invalid registration: short password\n        resp = self.register_user(\"user1@example.com\", \"123\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # Valid registration\n        resp = self.register_user(\"user1@example.com\", \"password1\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        # Duplicate registration\n        resp = self.register_user(\"user1@example.com\", \"password1\")\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # Login with wrong password\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'email': \"user1@example.com\",\n            'password': \"wrongpass\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 401)\n        # Login with correct password\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/login', json={\n            'email': \"user1@example.com\",\n            'password': \"password1\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"token\", json.loads(resp.data))\n\n    def test_jwt_auth_required(self):\n        # Login as admin\n        token = self.login_user(ADMIN_EMAIL, \"admin123\")\n        # Create product (valid)\n        resp = self.create_product(token, name=\"Product A\", price=20.0, stock=10)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 201)\n        pid = json.loads(resp.data)['id']\n        # Create product (invalid: negative price)\n        resp = self.create_product(token, name=\"Product B\", price=-5, stock=5)\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # List products\n        resp = self.app.get('/api/products')\n        products = json.loads(resp.data)\n        self.assertEqual(len(products), 1)\n        # Update product\n        resp = self.app.put(f'/api/admin/products/{pid}', json={\n            \"name\": \"Product A+\",\n            \"price\": 25.0\n        }, headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Delete product\n        resp = self.app.delete(f'/api/admin/products/{pid}', headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 200)\n        # Get deleted product\n        resp = self.app.get(f'/api/products/{pid}')\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 404)\n\n    def test_order_workflow(self):\n        # Place order with invalid product\n        resp = self.app.post('/api/orders', json={\n            \"items\": [{\"product_id\": 9999, \"quantity\": 1}],\n            \"payment_method\": \"paypal\"\n        }, headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"})\n        self.assertEqual(resp.status_code, 400)\n        # \"sqlite:///ecommerce.db\")\napp.config['SQLALCHEMY_TRACK_MODIFICATIONS'] = False\napp.config['SECRET_KEY'] = SECRET_KEY\n\ndb = SQLAlchemy(app)\nbcrypt = Bcrypt(app)\n\n# --- Models ---\n\nclass User(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    email = db.Column(db.String(120), unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = db.Column(db.String(128), nullable=False)\n    is_admin = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=False)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n\n    def verify_password(self, password):\n        return bcrypt.check_password_hash(self.password_hash, password)\n\nclass Product(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    name = db.Column(db.String(120), nullable=False)\n    description = db.Column(db.Text, nullable=True)\n    price = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n    image_url = db.Column(db.String(255), nullable=True)\n    stock = db.Column(db.Integer, default=0)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n\nclass Order(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    user_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('user.id'), nullable=False)\n    total = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n    status = db.Column(db.String(50), default=\"pending\")  # pending, paid, shipped, delivered, cancelled\n    payment_method = db.Column(db.String(50), nullable=False)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    items = db.relationship('OrderItem', backref='order', lazy=True)\n\nclass OrderItem(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    order_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('order.id'), nullable=False)\n    product_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('product.id'), nullable=False)\n    quantity = db.Column(db.Integer, nullable=False)\n    price = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n\n# --- Utility Functions ---\n\ndef create_jwt(user):\n    payload = {\n        \"user_id\": user.id,\n        \"email\": user.email,\n        \"is_admin\": user.is_admin,\n        \"exp\": datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=JWT_EXPIRY_MINUTES)\n    }\n    return jwt.encode(payload, SECRET_KEY, algorithm=\"HS256\")\n\ndef decode_jwt(token):\n    try:\n        return jwt.decode(token, SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[\"HS256\"])\n    except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:\n        return None\n    except jwt.InvalidTokenError:\n        return None\n\ndef login_required(f):\n    @wraps(f)\n    def decorated(*args, **kwargs):\n        header = request.headers.get('Authorization')\n        if not header or not header.startswith(\"Bearer \"):\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Missing or invalid token\"}), 401\n        token = header.split(\" \")[1]\n        data = decode_jwt(token)\n        if not data:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid or expired token\"}), 401\n        request.user = data\n        return f(*args, **kwargs)\n    return decorated\n\ndef admin_required(f):\n    @wraps(f)\n    def decorated(*args, **kwargs):\n        if not getattr(request, 'user', None) or not request.user.get('is_admin'):\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Admin access required\"}), 403\n        return f(*args, **kwargs)\n    return decorated\n\n# --- Routes ---\n\n@app.route('/api/register', methods=['POST'])\ndef register():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    email = data.get(\"email\", \"\").strip().lower()\n    password = data.get(\"password\", \"\")\n    if not email or not password or len(password) < 6:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid email or password\"}), 400\n    if User.query.filter_by(email=email).first():\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Email already registered\"}), 400\n    user = User(\n        email=email,\n        password_hash=bcrypt.generate_password_hash(password).decode('utf-8'),\n        is_admin=(email == ADMIN_EMAIL)\n    )\n    db.session.add(user)\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Registration successful\"}), 201\n\n@app.route('/api/login', methods=['POST'])\ndef login():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    email = data.get(\"email\", \"\").strip().lower()\n    password = data.get(\"password\", \"\")\n    user = User.query.filter_by(email=email).first()\n    if not user or not user.verify_password(password):\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid credentials\"}), 401\n    token = create_jwt(user)\n    return jsonify({\"token\": token})\n\n@app.route('/api/products', methods=['GET'])\ndef list_products():\n    products = Product.query.all()\n    return jsonify([{\n        \"id\": p.id,\n        \"name\": p.name,\n        \"description\": p.description,\n        \"price\": p.price,\n        \"image_url\": p.image_url,\n        \"stock\": p.stock\n    } for p in products])\n\n@app.route('/api/products/<int:product_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef get_product(product_id):\n    p = Product.query.get_or_404(product_id)\n    return jsonify({\n        \"id\": p.id,\n        \"name\": p.name,\n        \"description\": p.description,\n        \"price\": p.price,\n        \"image_url\": p.image_url,\n        \"stock\": p.stock\n    })\n\n# --- Admin Product Management ---\n\n@app.route('/api/admin/products', methods=['POST'])\n@login_required\n@admin_required\ndef create_product():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    name = data.get(\"name\", \"\").strip()\n    price = data.get(\"price\")\n    stock = data.get(\"stock\", 0)\n    if not name or price is None or price < 0 or stock < 0:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid product data\"}), 400\n    product = Product(\n        name=name,\n        description=data.get(\"description\", \"\"),\n        price=price,\n        image_url=data.get(\"image_url\", \"\"),\n        stock=stock\n    )\n    db.session.add(product)\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Product created\", \"id\": product.id}), 201\n\n@app.route('/api/admin/products/<int:product_id>', methods=['PUT'])\n@login_required\n@admin_required\ndef update_product(product_id):\n    product = Product.query.get_or_404(product_id)\n    data = request.get_json()\n    name = data.get(\"name\")\n    if name is not None:\n        product.name = name.strip()\n    if \"description\" in data:\n        product.description = data[\"description\"]\n    if \"price\" in data:\n        price = data[\"price\"]\n        if price is not None and price >= 0:\n            product.price = price\n        else:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid price\"}), 400\n    if \"image_url\" in data:\n        product.image_url = data[\"image_url\"]\n    if \"stock\" in data:\n        stock = data[\"stock\"]\n        if stock is not None and stock >= 0:\n            product.stock = stock\n        else:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid stock\"}), 400\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Product updated\"})\n\n@app.route('/api/admin/products/<int:product_id>', methods=['DELETE'])\n@login_required\n@admin_required\ndef delete_product(product_id):\n    product = Product.query.get_or_404(product_id)\n    db.session.delete(product)\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Product deleted\"})\n\n# --- Orders (Checkout) ---\n\n@app.route('/api/orders', methods=['POST'])\n@login_required\ndef create_order():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    items = data.get(\"items\", [])\n    payment_method = data.get(\"payment_method\", \"\")\n    if not items or payment_method not in [\"credit_card\", \"paypal\", \"stripe\"]:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid order data\"}), 400\n\n    total = 0\n    order_items = []\n    for item in items:\n        product = Product.query.get(item.get(\"product_id\"))\n        quantity = item.get(\"quantity\", 0)\n        if not product or quantity <= 0 or product.stock < quantity:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid product or insufficient stock\"}), 400\n        total += product.price * quantity\n        order_items.append((product, quantity))\n\n    # Mock payment processing\n    payment_success = mock_payment(payment_method, total)\n    if not payment_success:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Payment failed\"}), 402\n\n    order = Order(\n        user_id=request.user[\"user_id\"],\n        total=total,\n        status=\"paid\",\n        payment_method=payment_method\n    )\n    db.session.add(order)\n    db.session.flush()  # Get order.id\n\n    for product, quantity in order_items:\n        db.session.add(OrderItem(\n            order_id=order.id,\n            product_id=product.id,\n            quantity=quantity,\n            price=product.price\n        ))\n        product.stock -= quantity\n\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Order placed\", \"order_id\": order.id})\n\ndef mock_payment(method, amount):\n    # In production, integrate Stripe/PayPal SDKs here\n    return True  # Always succeeds for demo\n\n@app.route('/api/orders', methods=['GET'])\ndef health():\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"ok\"})\n\n@app.before_request\ndef enforce_https():\n    # For AWS/production, ensure HTTPS (remove for local dev)\n    if unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = db.Column(db.String(128), nullable=False)\n    is_admin = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=False)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n\n    def verify_password(self, password):\n        return bcrypt.check_password_hash(self.password_hash, password)\n\nclass Product(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    name = db.Column(db.String(120), nullable=False)\n    description = db.Column(db.Text, nullable=True)\n    price = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n    image_url = db.Column(db.String(255), nullable=True)\n    stock = db.Column(db.Integer, default=0)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n\nclass Order(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    user_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('user.id'), nullable=False)\n    total = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n    status = db.Column(db.String(50), default=\"pending\")  # pending, paid, shipped, delivered, cancelled\n    payment_method = db.Column(db.String(50), nullable=False)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    items = db.relationship('OrderItem', backref='order', lazy=True, cascade=\"all, delete-orphan\")\n\nclass OrderItem(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    order_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('order.id'), nullable=False)\n    product_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('product.id'), nullable=False)\n    quantity = db.Column(db.Integer, nullable=False)\n    price = db.Column(db.Float, nullable=False)\n\n# --- Utility Functions ---\n\ndef create_jwt(user):\n    payload = {\n        \"user_id\": user.id,\n        \"email\": user.email,\n        \"is_admin\": user.is_admin,\n        \"exp\": datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=JWT_EXPIRY_MINUTES)\n    }\n    return jwt.encode(payload, SECRET_KEY, algorithm=\"HS256\")\n\ndef decode_jwt(token):\n    try:\n        return jwt.decode(token, SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[\"HS256\"])\n    except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:\n        return None\n    except jwt.InvalidTokenError:\n        return None\n\ndef login_required(f):\n    @wraps(f)\n    def decorated(*args, **kwargs):\n        header = request.headers.get('Authorization', '')\n        if not header.startswith(\"Bearer \"):\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Missing or invalid token\"}), 401\n        token = header.split(\" \")[1]\n        data = decode_jwt(token)\n        if not data:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid or expired token\"}), 401\n        request.user = data\n        return f(*args, **kwargs)\n    return decorated\n\ndef admin_required(f):\n    @wraps(f)\n    def decorated(*args, **kwargs):\n        if not getattr(request, 'user', None) or not request.user.get('is_admin'):\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Admin access required\"}), 403\n        return f(*args, **kwargs)\n    return decorated\n\ndef validate_email(email):\n    import re\n    return re.match(r\"[^@]+@[^@]+\\.[^@]+\", email)\n\n# --- HTTPS Enforcement (for validate_email(email):\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid email or password\"}), 400\n    if User.query.filter_by(email=email).first():\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Email already registered\"}), 400\n    user = User(\n        email=email,\n        password_hash=bcrypt.generate_password_hash(password).decode('utf-8'),\n        is_admin=(email == ADMIN_EMAIL)\n    )\n methods=['PUT'])\n@login_required\n@admin_required\ndef update_product(product_id):\n    product = Product.query.get_or_404(product_id)\n    data = request.get_json()\n    if \"name\" in data:\n    product.description = data[\"description\"]\n    if \"price\" in data:\n        price = data[\"price\"]\n        if price is None or price < 0:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid price\"}), 400\n        product.price = price\n    if \"image_url\" in data:\n        product.image_url = data[\"image_url\"]\n    if \"stock\" in data:\n        stock = data[\"stock\"]\n        if ---\n\n@app.route('/api/orders', methods=['POST'])\n@login_required\ndef create_order():\n    data = request.get_json()\n    items = data.get(\"items\", [])\n    payment_method = = 0\n    order_items = []\n    for item in items:\n        product = Product.query.get(item.get(\"product_id\"))\n        quantity = item.get(\"quantity\", 0)\n        if not product or quantity <= 0 or product.stock < quantity:\n            return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid product or insufficient stock\"}), 400\n        total += product.price * quantity\n        order_items.append((product, db.session.flush()  # To get order.id before commit\n\n    for product, quantity in order_items:\n        db.session.add(OrderItem(\n            order_id=order.id,\n            product_id=product.id,\n            quantity=quantity,\n            price=product.price\n        ))\n        product.stock -= quantity\n\n    db.session.commit()\n    return jsonify({\"message\": \"Order placed\", \"order_id\": order.id})\n\ndef mock_payment(method, amount):\n    # In production, integrate Stripe/PayPal SDKs here\n    return True  # Always succeeds for     is_admin=True\n        )\n        db.session.add(admin)\n        db.session.commit()\n        print(f\"Admin user created: {ADMIN_EMAIL} / admin123\")\n\n# --- Main Entrypoint ---\n\nif __name__ json.loads(resp3.get_data(as_text=True))[\"id\"]\n\n        # Place order\n        resp4 = self.app.post('/api/orders', data=json.dumps({\n            \"items\": [{\"product_id\": prod_id, \"quantity\": 1}],\n            \"payment_method\": \"paypal\"\n        }), content_type='application/json', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"\n        })\n        order_id = json.loads(resp4.get_data(as_text=True))[\"order_id\"]\n\n        # Admin: get all orders\n        resp5 = self.app.get('/api/admin/orders', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {admin_token}\"\n        })\n        orders = json.loads(resp5.get_data(as_text=True))\n        self.assertEqual(len(orders), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(orders[0][\"id\"], order_id)\n        self.assertEqual(orders[0][\"status\"], \"paid\")\n\n        # Admin: update order status\n        resp6 = self.app.put(f'/api/admin/orders/{order_id}', data=json.dumps({\n            \"status\": \"shipped\"\n        }), content_type='application/json', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {admin_token}\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp6.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertIn(\"Order status updated\", resp6.get_data(as_text=True))\n\n        # Admin: update order status to invalid value\n        resp7 = self.app.put(f'/api/admin/orders/{order_id}', data=json.dumps({\n            \"status\": \"unknown\"\n        }), content_type='application/json', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {admin_token}\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp7.status_code, 400)\n\n        # Non-admin cannot access admin endpoints\n        resp8 = self.app.get('/api/admin/orders', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp8.status_code, 403)\n\n        resp9 = self.app.put(f'/api/admin/orders/{order_id}', data=json.dumps({\n            \"status\": \"delivered\"\n        }), content_type='application/json', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp9.status_code, 403)\n\n    def and login user\n        self.register_user(\"expire@test.com\", \"expire123\")\n        resp = self.login_user(\"expire@test.com\", \"expire123\")\n        token = json.loads(resp.get_data(as_text=True))[\"token\"]\n\n        # Tamper with token to simulate expiry\n        payload = jwt.decode(token, SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[\"HS256\"])\n        payload[\"exp\"] = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(minutes=1)\n        expired_token = jwt.encode(payload, SECRET_KEY, algorithm=\"HS256\")\n\n        resp2 = self.app.get('/api/orders', headers={\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {expired_token}\"\n        })\n        self.assertEqual(resp2.status_code, 401)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
